; Type OTHER can be used in User Fixes.txt for obstructions and other non-navigation items in Tracons.

; Recognized lat/long formats such as N35W141, 35N141W, 3500N/14100W, etc.
;   should NOT be defined as a Fix ID.

; Duplicate IDs not allowed.
; Single character fix ID not allowed.
; Fix ID 'XXX' not allowed.
; Airport IDs starting with a digit work so far.

; Gave up on keeping this file sorted.  Also nice to have fixes in a procedure together for revisions.
; Program sorts the fixes as necessary and reports/ignores duplicates.
